<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">terwilen</i>, a shortening of <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:ter.html>ter</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wilen.html>wilen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">at the <a href = vnd.unilang:moment.html>moment</a> that</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. See also <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wijl.html>wijl</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Conjunction">Conjunction</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:terwijl.html>terwijl</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>while, during the same time that</li>
<li>whereas
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:tussen.html>Tussen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geslachten.html>geslachten</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bestaat.html>bestaat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:groot.html>groot</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verschil.html>verschil</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:gewicht.html>gewicht</a>; <a href = vnd.unilang:mannetjes.html>mannetjes</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wegen.html>wegen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gemiddeld.html>gemiddeld</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ongeveer.html>ongeveer</a> 100 gram, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:terwijl.html>terwijl</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:vrouwtjes.html>vrouwtjes</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tot.html>tot</a> 160 gram <a href = vnd.unilang:kunnen.html>kunnen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wegen.html>wegen</a>.</i>
<dl><dd>Between the sexes there exists a big difference in weight; the males weigh on the average approximately 100 grams, <i>whereas</i> the females can weigh up to 160 grams.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Voegwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:voegwoord.html>Voegwoord</a></i></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:testament.html>testament</a> (3984)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:testament.html>testament</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href = vnd.unilang:testament.html>testament</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">testāmentum</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">the publication of a will, a will, <a href = vnd.unilang:testament.html>testament</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:testament.html>testament</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:testamenten.html>testamenten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:testament.html>testamentje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">law</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href="English"><a href = vnd.unilang:testament.html>testament</a></a>, last will</li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">toghel</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:teugel.html>teugel</a></i>,<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup> from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*tugilaz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">rein on a horse</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>,<sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-2"> | 2 | </a></sup> whence also Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">tygill</i>, Old English <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">tygel</i>, Old High German <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">zugil</i> (German <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Zügel</i>). <p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:tevreden.html>tevreden</a></i>. <head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:teweegbrengen.html>teweegbrengen</a> (46320)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From the preposition <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a></i> + an archaic inflection of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:weg.html>weg</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">way</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:brengen.html>brengen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to bring</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***tewerkstellen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:tewerkstellen.html>tewerkstellen</a> (122910)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:werk.html>werk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:stellen.html>stellen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to put to work</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tewerkstellen.html>tewerkstellen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to employ, to hire <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to give work to someone</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***thalamus.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:thalamus.html>thalamus</a> (79008)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/New_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:New Latin">New Latin</a></span></span>, from <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:thalamus.html>thalamus</a></i>, from <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">θάλαμος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">thálamos</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">an inner chamber, a bedroom, a <a href = vnd.unilang:bed.html>bed</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<div class="sister-wikipedia sister-project noprint floatright" style="border: 1px solid aaa; font-size: 90%; background: f9f9f9; width: 250px; padding: 4px; text-align: left;"><div style="float: left;"><div class="floatnone"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/44px-Wikipedia-logo.png" decoding="async" width="44" height="44" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/66px-Wikipedia-logo.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/88px-Wikipedia-logo.png 2x" data-file-width="200" data-file-height="200" /></div></div><div style="margin-left: 60px;">English Wikipedia <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> an article on:<div style="margin-left: 10px;"><b class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/thalamus" class="extiw" title="w:thalamus"><a href = vnd.unilang:thalamus.html>thalamus</a></a></b></div></div><span class="interProject"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/thalamus" class="extiw" title="w:thalamus">Wikipedia </a></span></div>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:thalamus.html>thalamus</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">thalami</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">thalamuses</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">anatomy</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Either of two large, ovoid structures of grey matter within the forebrain that relay sensory impulses to the cerebral cortex.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">botany</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The receptacle of a flower; a torus.</li>
<li>A thallus.</li>
<li>An inner room or nuptial chamber.</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:thalamus.html>thalamus</a></b>
</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:anatomie.html>anatomie</a>)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:grijze.html>grijze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:stof.html>stof</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> tussenhersenen</li></ol>
<div style="clear:both;"></div>
</body>

<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bedankt.html>bedankt</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dank.html>dank</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dank.html>dank</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:u.html>u</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dank.html>dank</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wel.html>wel</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dank.html>dank</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:u.html>u</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wel.html>wel</a></span></span></dd>

***thanksgiving.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:thanksgiving.html>thanksgiving</a> (4796)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:thanks.html>thanks</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">giving</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:thanksgiving.html>thanksgiving</a></strong> (<i>countable and uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:thanksgivings.html>thanksgivings</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>an expression of gratitude.
<ul><li><b>1918</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Edgar_Rice_Burroughs" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Edgar Rice Burroughs"><a href = vnd.unilang:edgar.html>Edgar</a> Rice Burroughs</a>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Land_That_Time_Forgot_(novel)" class="extiw" title="w:The Land That Time Forgot (novel)">The <a href = vnd.unilang:land.html>Land</a> That Time <a href = vnd.unilang:forgot.html>Forgot</a></a> Chapter IV
<dl><dd>The waters grew suddenly lighter, and my <a href = vnd.unilang:spirits.html>spirits</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:rose.html>rose</a> accordingly. I shouted down to those below that I saw daylight ahead, and a great shout of <b><a href = vnd.unilang:thanksgiving.html>thanksgiving</a></b> reverberated through the ship. A <a href = vnd.unilang:moment.html>moment</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:later.html>later</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> emerged into sunlit water, and immediately I raised the periscope and looked about <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> upon the strangest landscape I <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> ever seen.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>a short prayer <a href = vnd.unilang:said.html>said</a> at meals; <a href = vnd.unilang:grace.html>grace</a>, a benediction.</li>
<li>A public celebration in acknowledgement of divine favour.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1907</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Harold_Edward_Bindloss" class="extiw" title="w:Harold Edward Bindloss">Harold Bindloss</a>,  chapter 20, in  <cite>The Dust of Conflict</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://openlibrary.org/works/OL4429277W">[1]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:hester.html>Hester</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:earle.html>Earle</a> and <a href = vnd.unilang:violet.html>Violet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wayne.html>Wayne</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> moving about the aisle with bundles of wheat-ears and streamers of ivy, for the harvest <b><a href = vnd.unilang:thanksgiving.html>thanksgiving</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> shortly to be celebrated, while the vicar stood waiting for their directions on the chancel <a href = vnd.unilang:steps.html>steps</a> with a great handful of crimson gladioli.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
</body>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a>(e)hande</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a>(e)hant</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">at</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">hand</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">hand</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. ***thatch.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:thatch.html>thatch</a> (42960)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Variant of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">thack</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">thache, thach</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">þæc</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">roof-covering</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*þaką</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">covering</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from (o-grade of) <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*(s)teg-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cover</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Icelandic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Icelandic language">Icelandic</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="is">þak</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dak.html>dak</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Dach</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Norwegian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Norwegian language">Norwegian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="no"><a href = vnd.unilang:tak.html>tak</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv"><a href = vnd.unilang:tak.html>tak</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">tag</i>; and with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:toga.html>toga</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Albanian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Albanian language">Albanian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sq">thak</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">awn, beard, pin, peg, tassel, fringe</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lithuanian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Lithuanian language">Lithuanian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lt">stogas</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">roof</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Related to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">τέγος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tégos</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">roof</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">στέγη</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stégē</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">roof</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. See also English <span class="Latn" lang="en">deech</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">deck</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:thatch.html>thatch</a></strong> (<i>countable and uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">thatches</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Straw, <a href = vnd.unilang:rushes.html>rushes</a>, or similar, used for making or covering the roofs of buildings, or of stacks of hay or grain.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">Caribbean</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Any of several <a href = vnd.unilang:kinds.html>kinds</a> of palm, the leaves of which are used for thatching.</li>
<li>A buildup of cut grass, stolons or other material on the soil in a lawn.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">by extension</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Any straw-like material, such as a person's hair.
<ul><li><b>2008</b>, Wallace Madding, <i>The Country Club Killings: A Montana Story</i> (page 21)
<dl><dd>An outgoing, story-telling Irishman from <a href = vnd.unilang:butte.html>Butte</a>, Montana, with his <b><a href = vnd.unilang:thatch.html>thatch</a></b> of red hair and sandpapered face, <a href = vnd.unilang:matt.html>Matt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> the quintessential imp.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">straw for covering roofs or stacks</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">haulm</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">thecchen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">þeċċan</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">þeċċean</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*þakjaną</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy"><a href = vnd.unilang:dekken.html>dekke</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dekken.html>dekken</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">decken</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">tække</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">täcka</i>. Alteration of vowel after Middle English perhaps due to the above noun.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:thatch.html>thatch</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">thatches</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">thatching</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">thatched</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>To cover the roof with straw, <a href = vnd.unilang:reed.html>reed</a>, leaves, etc.</li></ol>
</body>

***theater.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:theater.html>theater</a> (2652)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">theatre</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">theatrum</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">θέατρον</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">théatron</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a place for viewing</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">θεάομαι</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">theáomai</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to see", "to watch", "to observe</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:theater.html>theater</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:theaters.html>theaters</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:theatertje.html>theatertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:theater.html>theater</a></span> (<i>US</i>), <span class="Latn" lang="en">theatre</span> (<i>Commonwealth</i>): either drama, the art form, or a drama <a href = vnd.unilang:theater.html>theater</a> (building)</li></ol>

***thee.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:thee.html>thee</a> (1189)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowing from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Malay_language" class="extiw" title="w:Malay language">Malay</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="ms">teh</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Southern_Min" class="extiw" title="w:Southern Min"><a href = vnd.unilang:min.html>Min</a> Nan</a></span> <i class="Hani mention" lang="nan">茶</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="nan-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tê</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The "-h-" <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a Faux-Greek spelling (compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Greek_language" class="extiw" title="w:Greek language">Greek</a></span> <i class="Grek mention" lang="el">τσάι</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="el-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tsái</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>).
</p>

<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:thee.html>thee</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">tea</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:doek.html>doek</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cloth</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:theemuts.html>theemuts</a> (87384)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:thee.html>thee</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">tea</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:muts.html>muts</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:toque.html>toque</a>, brimless cap</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:theemuts.html>theemuts</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:theemuts.html>theemutsen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:theemuts.html>theemutsje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>tea cosy <span class="defdate">[from late 19th c.]</span>
<ul><li><b>1896</b> January 1, "<a href = vnd.unilang:ontvreemden.html>Ontvreemde</a> of <a href = vnd.unilang:vermiste.html>vermiste</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voorwerpen.html>voorwerpen</a>", <i>Haarlem's <a href = vnd.unilang:dagblad.html>Dagblad</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:vol.html>Vol</a>. 13, No. 3834, page 2.
<dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="nl">Den 23 Dec. jl. <a href = vnd.unilang:heeft.html>heeft</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zekere.html>zekere</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ella.html>Ella</a> Starck 18 <a href = vnd.unilang:jaren.html>jaren</a>, wonende <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> Nijmegen, <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> 's Hertogenbosch <a href = vnd.unilang:door.html>door</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:oplichting.html>oplichting</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verkregen.html>verkregen</a>; <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span> 1 <a href = vnd.unilang:beige.html>beige</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:theemuts.html>theemuts</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:blauw.html>blauw</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:goud.html>goud</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bewerkt.html>bewerkt</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:afgewerkt.html>afgewerkt</a>; <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span></span><dl><dd><small>(please add an English translation of this quote)</small></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
